                function initTimes () {
                    for (let hour = 7; hour <= 24; hour++) {
                        for (let minute = 0; minute < 60; minute += 30) {
                            // var hourStr = hour;
                             const timeString = `${hour.toString().padStart(2, "0")}:${minute
                                .toString()
                                .padStart(2, "0")}`;
                                if(timeString == '24:30'){
                                    continue
                                }
                                times.push(timeString);
                            
                        }
                    }
                    for (let hour = 0; hour < 7; hour++) {
                        for (let minute = 0; minute < 60; minute += 30) {
                            const timeString = `${hour.toString().padStart(2, "0")}:${minute
                                .toString()
                                .padStart(2, "0")}`;
                            times.push(timeString);
                        }
                    }

                // 计算时间差
                function calculateHourDifference (start, end) {
                    // 解析时间（小时和分钟）
                    const [startHour, startMinute] = start.split(":").map(Number);
                    const [endHour, endMinute] = end.split(":").map(Number);
                    // 转换为分钟数
                    // 检查结束时间是否早于开始时间

                    let startTotalMinutes = startHour * 60 + startMinute;
                    let endTotalMinutes = endHour * 60 + endMinute;
                    if (endTotalMinutes < startTotalMinutes) {
                        return null;
                    }
                    // 计算分钟差并转换为小时（0.5表示30分钟）
                    const minuteDifference = endTotalMinutes - startTotalMinutes;
                    return minuteDifference / 60;
                }
                function isValidDate (date) {
                    return date instanceof Date && !isNaN(date.getTime());

                            $("#workTimes_" + index).val(diff);
                        });

                function saveForm (callback) {
                    var formdata = form.val("beanForm1");
                    var val1 = form.verifyForm("beanForm1");
                    if (!val1) {
                        return;
                    }
                    var val2 = form.verifyForm("personWorkTimesItemForm");
                    if (!val2) {
                        return;
                    }
                    var personWorkTimesItemDtoList = personWorkTimesItemTable.val(
                        "#dytable_personWorkTimesItemTable"
                    );
                    if (personWorkTimesItemDtoList.length == 0) {
                        notice.warning("请至少添加一条工时内容信息！");
                        return;
                    }

                    // personWorkTimesItemDtoList.forEach((item, index) => {
                    //     item.itemBeginDate = formdata.workDate + " " + item.itemBeginDate;
                    //     item.itemEndDate = formdata.workDate + " " + item.itemEndDate;
                    // });
                    formdata.personWorkTimesItemDtoList = personWorkTimesItemDtoList;

                    method
                        .postCheckHave({
                            data: {
                                id: formdata.id,
                                applyUserId: formdata.applyUserId,
                                workDate: formdata.workDate,
                            },
                        })
                        .then(function (res) {
                            if (res.data == "") {
                                method
                                    .postBean({
                                        data: formdata,
                                        timeout: 60 * 1000,
                                    })
                                    .then(function (resp) {
                                        if (resp.code == "1001") {
                                            $("#id").val(resp.data.id);
                                            notice.success("保存成功！");
                                            if (typeof callback == "function") {
                                                callback(resp.data);
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            notice.error("保存失败");
                                        }
                                    });
                            } else {
                                notice.warning(res.data);
                                return;
                            }
                        });
                }

                // 保存
                $("#save").click(function () {
                    saveForm();
                });

                //生效
                $("#takeEffect").click(function () {

                    var personWorkTimesItemList = personWorkTimesItemTable.val("#dytable_personWorkTimesItemTable");

                    $.each(personWorkTimesItemList, function (index, item) {
                        // 如果选测试实验和合成实验就要是必填 领导要求不能单独做实验
                        if ((item.workForm == '9' || item.workForm == '10') && item.coCompletionPersonId == '') {
                            notice.error("请填写共同完成人");
                            return;
                        } else {
                            //设置生效状态
                            form.val("beanForm1", {
                                effectState: "1",
                            });

                            saveForm(function () {
                                layui.personWorkTimes_list.editSuccess();
                            });
                        }
                    });


                });
                //关闭页面
                $("#closeForm").click(function () {
                    layer.confirm("确定关闭页面？", function (index) {
                        layer.close(index);
                        layui.personWorkTimes_list.editSuccess();
                    });
                });

                DigitalFormat = function (my) {
                    if (typeof my != undefined) {
                        var val = my.value;
                        if (isNaN(val)) {
                            val = "0.00";
                        }
                        if (val != "") {
                            var m = Math.round(val * 100) / 100;
                            if (parseInt(m) == m) {
                                m = m + ".00";
                            } else {
                                var n1 = m.toString().length;
                                var n2 = parseInt(m).toString().length;
                                if (n1 - n2 == 2) {
                                    m = m + "0";
                                }
                            }
                            if (m < 0) {
                                m = "0.00";
                            }
                            my.value = m;
                        } else {
                            my.value = "0.00";
                        }
                    }
                };

                exports("personWorkTimes_form", {});
            }
        );

                function initTimes () {
                    for (let hour = 7; hour <= 24; hour++) {
                        for (let minute = 0; minute < 60; minute += 30) {
                            // var hourStr = hour;
                             const timeString = `${hour.toString().padStart(2, "0")}:${minute
                                .toString()
                                .padStart(2, "0")}`;
                                if(timeString == '24:30'){
                                    continue
                                }
                                times.push(timeString);
                            
                        }
                    }
                    for (let hour = 0; hour < 7; hour++) {
                        for (let minute = 0; minute < 60; minute += 30) {
                            const timeString = `${hour.toString().padStart(2, "0")}:${minute
                                .toString()
                                .padStart(2, "0")}`;
                            times.push(timeString);
                        }
                    }
                }

                // 计算时间差
                function calculateHourDifference (start, end) {
                    // 解析时间（小时和分钟）
                    const [startHour, startMinute] = start.split(":").map(Number);
                    const [endHour, endMinute] = end.split(":").map(Number);
                    // 转换为分钟数
                    // 检查结束时间是否早于开始时间

                    let startTotalMinutes = startHour * 60 + startMinute;
                    let endTotalMinutes = endHour * 60 + endMinute;
                    if (endTotalMinutes < startTotalMinutes) {
                        return null;
                    }
                    // 计算分钟差并转换为小时（0.5表示30分钟）
                    const minuteDifference = endTotalMinutes - startTotalMinutes;
                    return minuteDifference / 60;
                }
                function isValidDate (date) {
                    return date instanceof Date && !isNaN(date.getTime());

                        });
                        
                        layui.form.on("select(itemBeginDate_" + index + ")", function (data) {
                                var beginTime = data.value;

                function saveForm (callback) {
                    var formdata = form.val("beanForm1");
                    var val1 = form.verifyForm("beanForm1");
                    if (!val1) {
                        return;
                    }
                    var val2 = form.verifyForm("personWorkTimesItemForm");
                    if (!val2) {
                        return;
                    }
                    var personWorkTimesItemDtoList = personWorkTimesItemTable.val(
                        "#dytable_personWorkTimesItemTable"
                    );
                    if (personWorkTimesItemDtoList.length == 0) {
                        notice.warning("请至少添加一条工时内容信息！");
                        return;
                    }

                    // personWorkTimesItemDtoList.forEach((item, index) => {
                    //     item.itemBeginDate = formdata.workDate + " " + item.itemBeginDate;
                    //     item.itemEndDate = formdata.workDate + " " + item.itemEndDate;
                    // });
                    formdata.personWorkTimesItemDtoList = personWorkTimesItemDtoList;

                    method
                        .postCheckHave({
                            data: {
                                id: formdata.id,
                                applyUserId: formdata.applyUserId,
                                workDate: formdata.workDate,
                            },
                        })
                        .then(function (res) {
                            if (res.data == "") {
                                method
                                    .postBean({
                                        data: formdata,
                                        timeout: 60 * 1000,
                                    })
                                    .then(function (resp) {
                                        if (resp.code == "1001") {
                                            $("#id").val(resp.data.id);
                                            notice.success("保存成功！");
                                            if (typeof callback == "function") {
                                                callback(resp.data);
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            notice.error("保存失败");
                                        }
                                    });
                            } else {
                                notice.warning(res.data);
                                return;
                            }
                        });
                }

                // 保存
                $("#save").click(function () {
                    saveForm();
                });

                //生效
                $("#takeEffect").click(function () {

                    var personWorkTimesItemList = personWorkTimesItemTable.val("#dytable_personWorkTimesItemTable");

                    $.each(personWorkTimesItemList, function (index, item) {
                        // 如果选测试实验和合成实验就要是必填 领导要求不能单独做实验
                        if ((item.workForm == '9' || item.workForm == '10') && item.coCompletionPersonId == '') {
                            notice.error("请填写共同完成人");
                            return;
                        } else {
                            //设置生效状态
                            form.val("beanForm1", {
                                effectState: "1",
                            });

                            saveForm(function () {
                                layui.personWorkTimes_list.editSuccess();
                            });
                        }
                    });


                });
                //关闭页面
                $("#closeForm").click(function () {
                    layer.confirm("确定关闭页面？", function (index) {
                        layer.close(index);
                        layui.personWorkTimes_list.editSuccess();
                    });
                });

                DigitalFormat = function (my) {
                    if (typeof my != undefined) {
                        var val = my.value;
                        if (isNaN(val)) {
                            val = "0.00";
                        }
                        if (val != "") {
                            var m = Math.round(val * 100) / 100;
                            if (parseInt(m) == m) {
                                m = m + ".00";
                            } else {
                                var n1 = m.toString().length;
                                var n2 = parseInt(m).toString().length;
                                if (n1 - n2 == 2) {
                                    m = m + "0";
                                }
                            }
                            if (m < 0) {
                                m = "0.00";
                            }
                            my.value = m;
                        } else {
                            my.value = "0.00";
                        }
                    }
                };

                exports("personWorkTimes_form", {});
            }
        );
    };</script></div><span class="layui-layer-setwin"><a class="layui-layer-ico layui-layer-close layui-layer-close1" href="javascript:;"></a></span><span class="layui-layer-resize"></span></div>

  layui.use(['layer', 'frame', 'admin', 'flow', 'element','form','setter','bkadmin'], function () {
    var $ = layui.$,
      BK = layui.frame,
      admin = layui.admin,
      flow = layui.flow,
      setter = layui.setter,
      form=BK.form,
      bkadmin = layui.bkadmin,
      element = layui.element,
    layer = layui.layer;


    var queryArr = setter.admin['system.user.select.query'];
    // queryArr=[
    //   {type:"input",name:"name1",label:"范围"},
    //   {type:"select",name:"name2",label:"select",dicCode:"gyxm_zl"},
    //   {type:"radio",name:"name3",label:"radio",dicCode:"gyxm_zl"},
    //   {type:"checkbox",name:"name4",label:"checkbox",dicCode:"gyxm_zl"},
    // ]
    if(queryArr){
      queryArr=JSON.parse(queryArr)
      if (queryArr.length>0) {
      var sb='',dicArr=[]
      $(queryArr).each(function(index,item){
        var id=item.type+'_query_'+index
        sb+='  <div class="layui-col-md4">';
        sb+='     <label class="layui-form-label">'+item.label+'</label>';
        sb+='     <div class="layui-input-block">';
        if(item.type=='select'||item.type=='radio'||item.type=='checkbox'){
          sb+='       <div class="" id="'+id+'"></div>';
          item.id=id
          dicArr.push(item)
          }else{
            sb+='       <input name="'+item.name+'" maxlength="20" autocomplete="off" class="layui-input" />';
          }
       
        sb+='     </div>';
        sb+='   </div>';
      });
      $(".advanced_query_box .layui-form-item").append(sb)
      var asvIdArr=["#advanced_query_box1","#advanced_query_box2","#advanced_query_box3"]
      if(dicArr.length>0){
        $(dicArr).each(function(index,item){
          $(asvIdArr).each(function(index2,item2){
            bkadmin.getDic([
            {
              type: item.type,
              elem: item2+' #'+item.id,
              code: item.dicCode,
              fieldName: item.name,
              addAllOption: true,
              addAllOptionText: '全部'
            }
          ])
        })
      })
    }
 
    }
    }

    var search = layui.data('userSelect1-search')
    var range=setter.admin['system.userSelect1.search.range']
    if (typeof search.range === 'undefined') {
        layui.data('userSelect1-search', {
          key: 'range',
          value: range
        });
    }else{
      range=search.range
    }
      form.val("userSelect1SeachForm1", {
        range:range
      });

      form.on('select(range)', function(data){
        layui.data('userSelect1-search', {
          key: 'range',
          value: data.value
        });
      });      
      
      bkadmin.getDic([
        {
          type: "select",
          elem: "#job_title1",
          code: "job_title",
          fieldName: "title",
          disabled: false,
          required: true,
          addAllOption: true,
          addAllOptionText: '全部'
        },
        {
          type: "select",
          elem: "#job_title2",
          code: "job_title",
          fieldName: "title",
          disabled: false,
          required: true,
          addAllOption: true,
          addAllOptionText: '全部'
        },
        {
          type: "select",
          elem: "#job_title3",
          code: "job_title",
          fieldName: "title",
          disabled: false,
          required: true,
          addAllOption: true,
          addAllOptionText: '全部'
        }
      ])

    element.on('tab(user-select-tab)', function (e) {
      $(".bk-address-checked .bk-shrink-btn").parent().removeClass('open')
      $('.advanced_query_box').hide()
    });

    $(".bk-address-checked .bk-shrink-btn").click(function () {
      $(this).parent().toggleClass('open')
    })

    $(".user_advanced_query").click(function(){
      $(this).parents('.layui-form').find('.advanced_query_box').toggle()
    })

    $(".query-button").click(function(){
      $(this).parents('.layui-form').find('.advanced_query_box').hide()
    })


    $("#user_select_container_popup").on('click',function(e){
      if($(e.target).closest('.bk-grid-query').length==0){
        $('.advanced_query_box').hide()
      }
    })

    form.render()
  });

        layui.define(

            function (exports) {
                var $ = layui.$,
                    admin = layui.admin,
                    layer = layui.layer,
                    BK = layui.frame,
                    table = layui.frame.table,
                    notice = layui.frame.notice,
                    form = layui.frame.form,
                    element = layui.element,
                    smCovert = layui.smCovert,
                    laydate = layui.laydate,

                    moment = layui.moment,
                    workflow = bkadmin.workflow,
                    bkutil = layui.bkutil,
                    smConceal = layui.smConceal,
                    filedata = bkadmin.filedata,
                    exploreApprovalSelectIndex = layui.exploreApprovalSelectIndex,
                    kyProjectCardSelectIndex = layui.kyProjectCardSelectIndex;
                // 编辑时,需传入到filedata的contenId中
                var tid = param.id;
                var data = param.data;

                var method = BK.generate([
                    { name: "getUser", url: BK.config.api.admin + "/api/system/user/me" },
                    {
                        name: "getDicByCodes",
                        url: BK.config.api.admin + "/api/system/dictionary/getCode",
                    },
                    {
                        name: "getBean",

                            BK.config.api.project +

                laydate.render({
                    elem: ".date",
                });
                var times = [];
                function initTimes () {
                    for (let hour = 7; hour <= 24; hour++) {
                        for (let minute = 0; minute < 60; minute += 30) {
                            // var hourStr = hour;
                             const timeString = `${hour.toString().padStart(2, "0")}:${minute
                                .toString()
                                .padStart(2, "0")}`;
                                if(timeString == '24:30'){
                                    continue
                                }
                                times.push(timeString);
                            
                        }
                    }
                    for (let hour = 0; hour < 7; hour++) {
                        for (let minute = 0; minute < 60; minute += 30) {
                            const timeString = `${hour.toString().padStart(2, "0")}:${minute
                                .toString()
                                .padStart(2, "0")}`;
                            times.push(timeString);
                        }
                    }
                }

                // 计算时间差
                function calculateHourDifference (start, end) {
                    // 解析时间（小时和分钟）
                    const [startHour, startMinute] = start.split(":").map(Number);
                    const [endHour, endMinute] = end.split(":").map(Number);
                    // 转换为分钟数
                    // 检查结束时间是否早于开始时间

                    let startTotalMinutes = startHour * 60 + startMinute;
                    let endTotalMinutes = endHour * 60 + endMinute;
                    if (endTotalMinutes < startTotalMinutes) {
                        return null;
                    }
                    // 计算分钟差并转换为小时（0.5表示30分钟）
                    const minuteDifference = endTotalMinutes - startTotalMinutes;
                    return minuteDifference / 60;
                }

                    return date instanceof Date && !isNaN(date.getTime());

                function saveForm (callback) {
                    var formdata = form.val("beanForm1");
                    var val1 = form.verifyForm("beanForm1");
                    if (!val1) {
                        return;
                    }
                    var val2 = form.verifyForm("personWorkTimesItemForm");
                    if (!val2) {
                        return;
                    }
                    var personWorkTimesItemDtoList = personWorkTimesItemTable.val(
                        "#dytable_personWorkTimesItemTable"
                    );
                    if (personWorkTimesItemDtoList.length == 0) {
                        notice.warning("请至少添加一条工时内容信息！");
                        return;
                    }

                    // personWorkTimesItemDtoList.forEach((item, index) => {
                    //     item.itemBeginDate = formdata.workDate + " " + item.itemBeginDate;
                    //     item.itemEndDate = formdata.workDate + " " + item.itemEndDate;
                    // });
                    formdata.personWorkTimesItemDtoList = personWorkTimesItemDtoList;

                    method
                        .postCheckHave({
                            data: {
                                id: formdata.id,
                                applyUserId: formdata.applyUserId,
                                workDate: formdata.workDate,
                            },
                        })
                        .then(function (res) {
                            if (res.data == "") {
                                method
                                    .postBean({
                                        data: formdata,
                                        timeout: 60 * 1000,
                                    })
                                    .then(function (resp) {
                                        if (resp.code == "1001") {
                                            $("#id").val(resp.data.id);
                                            notice.success("保存成功！");
                                            if (typeof callback == "function") {
                                                callback(resp.data);
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            notice.error("保存失败");
                                        }
                                    });
                            } else {
                                notice.warning(res.data);
                                return;
                            }
                        });
                }

                // 保存
                $("#save").click(function () {
                    saveForm();
                });

                //生效
                $("#takeEffect").click(function () {

                    var personWorkTimesItemList = personWorkTimesItemTable.val("#dytable_personWorkTimesItemTable");

                    $.each(personWorkTimesItemList, function (index, item) {
                        // 如果选测试实验和合成实验就要是必填 领导要求不能单独做实验
                        if ((item.workForm == '9' || item.workForm == '10') && item.coCompletionPersonId == '') {
                            notice.error("请填写共同完成人");
                            return;
                        } else {
                            //设置生效状态
                            form.val("beanForm1", {
                                effectState: "1",
                            });

                            saveForm(function () {
                                layui.personWorkTimes_list.editSuccess();
                            });
                        }
                    });


                });
                //关闭页面
                $("#closeForm").click(function () {
                    layer.confirm("确定关闭页面？", function (index) {
                        layer.close(index);
                        layui.personWorkTimes_list.editSuccess();
                    });
                });

                DigitalFormat = function (my) {
                    if (typeof my != undefined) {
                        var val = my.value;
                        if (isNaN(val)) {
                            val = "0.00";
                        }
                        if (val != "") {
                            var m = Math.round(val * 100) / 100;
                            if (parseInt(m) == m) {
                                m = m + ".00";
                            } else {
                                var n1 = m.toString().length;
                                var n2 = parseInt(m).toString().length;
                                if (n1 - n2 == 2) {
                                    m = m + "0";
                                }
                            }
                            if (m < 0) {
                                m = "0.00";
                            }
                            my.value = m;
                        } else {
                            my.value = "0.00";
                        }
                    }
                };

                exports("personWorkTimes_form", {});
            }
        );

</div><script>
  layui.use(['layer', 'frame', 'admin', 'flow', 'element','form','setter','bkadmin'], function () {
    var $ = layui.$,
      BK = layui.frame,
      admin = layui.admin,
      flow = layui.flow,
      setter = layui.setter,
      form=BK.form,
      bkadmin = layui.bkadmin,
      element = layui.element,
    layer = layui.layer;


    var queryArr = setter.admin['system.user.select.query'];
    // queryArr=[
    //   {type:"input",name:"name1",label:"范围"},
    //   {type:"select",name:"name2",label:"select",dicCode:"gyxm_zl"},
    //   {type:"radio",name:"name3",label:"radio",dicCode:"gyxm_zl"},
    //   {type:"checkbox",name:"name4",label:"checkbox",dicCode:"gyxm_zl"},
    // ]
    if(queryArr){
      queryArr=JSON.parse(queryArr)
      if (queryArr.length>0) {
      var sb='',dicArr=[]
      $(queryArr).each(function(index,item){
        var id=item.type+'_query_'+index
        sb+='  <div class="layui-col-md4">';
        sb+='     <label class="layui-form-label">'+item.label+'</label>';
        sb+='     <div class="layui-input-block">';
        if(item.type=='select'||item.type=='radio'||item.type=='checkbox'){
          sb+='       <div class="" id="'+id+'"></div>';
          item.id=id
          dicArr.push(item)
          }else{
            sb+='       <input name="'+item.name+'" maxlength="20" autocomplete="off" class="layui-input" />';
          }
       
        sb+='     </div>';
        sb+='   </div>';
      });
      $(".advanced_query_box .layui-form-item").append(sb)
      var asvIdArr=["#advanced_query_box1","#advanced_query_box2","#advanced_query_box3"]
      if(dicArr.length>0){
        $(dicArr).each(function(index,item){
          $(asvIdArr).each(function(index2,item2){
            bkadmin.getDic([
            {
              type: item.type,
              elem: item2+' #'+item.id,
              code: item.dicCode,
              fieldName: item.name,
              addAllOption: true,
              addAllOptionText: '全部'
            }
          ])
        })
      })
    }
 
    }
    }

    var search = layui.data('userSelect1-search')
    var range=setter.admin['system.userSelect1.search.range']
    if (typeof search.range === 'undefined') {
        layui.data('userSelect1-search', {
          key: 'range',
          value: range
        });
    }else{
      range=search.range
    }
      form.val("userSelect1SeachForm1", {
        range:range
      });

      form.on('select(range)', function(data){
        layui.data('userSelect1-search', {
          key: 'range',
          value: data.value
        });
      });      
      
      bkadmin.getDic([
        {
          type: "select",
          elem: "#job_title1",
          code: "job_title",
          fieldName: "title",
          disabled: false,
          required: true,
          addAllOption: true,
          addAllOptionText: '全部'
        },
        {
          type: "select",
          elem: "#job_title2",
          code: "job_title",
          fieldName: "title",
          disabled: false,
          required: true,
          addAllOption: true,
          addAllOptionText: '全部'
        },
        {
          type: "select",
          elem: "#job_title3",
          code: "job_title",
          fieldName: "title",
          disabled: false,
          required: true,
          addAllOption: true,
          addAllOptionText: '全部'
        }
      ])

    element.on('tab(user-select-tab)', function (e) {
      $(".bk-address-checked .bk-shrink-btn").parent().removeClass('open')
      $('.advanced_query_box').hide()
    });

    $(".bk-address-checked .bk-shrink-btn").click(function () {
      $(this).parent().toggleClass('open')
    })

    $(".user_advanced_query").click(function(){
      $(this).parents('.layui-form').find('.advanced_query_box').toggle()
    })

    $(".query-button").click(function(){
      $(this).parents('.layui-form').find('.advanced_query_box').hide()
    })


    $("#user_select_container_popup").on('click',function(e){
      if($(e.target).closest('.bk-grid-query').length==0){
        $('.advanced_query_box').hide()
      }
    })

    form.render()
  });

</script></div>
<!-- SPECIFIC ID: #user_select_container_popup END -->
